## Domain Knowledge (LLM-generated)
**Domain**: population ecology / population dynamics
**Analysis**: This task models the population growth rate dP/dt as a function of time t and population P, which is the core problem of population dynamics. The relationship likely involves density-dependent growth with possible time-varying environmental effects.

**Common formula structures in this domain**:
- Exponential (Malthusian) growth: dP_dt = c0 * P (density-independent unlimited growth)
- Logistic growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) (density-dependent growth with carrying capacity)
- Gompertz growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * log(c1 / P) (growth decelerating logarithmically near capacity)
- Theta-logistic growth: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) (generalized logistic with shape parameter)
- Allee effect model: dP_dt = c0 * P * (P * c1 - 1) * (1 - c2 * P) (growth with minimum viable population)
- Logistic with harvesting: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) - c2 * P (logistic growth minus proportional removal)
- Logistic with constant harvesting: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) - c2 (logistic growth minus constant removal)
- Seasonal logistic: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P) * (1 + c2 * sin(c3 * t)) (logistic with periodic environmental forcing)
- Time-varying carrying capacity: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P * exp(c2 * t)) (logistic with shifting capacity)
- Richards growth model: dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**(c2)) * (c3)**(-1) (flexible sigmoidal growth)
- Beverton-Holt continuous: dP_dt = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (growth rate saturating at high density)
- Polynomial density dependence: dP_dt = c0 * P + c1 * P**2 + c2 * P**3 (general density-dependent expansion)
- Exponential with time decay: dP_dt = c0 * P * exp(c1 * t) (growth rate changing exponentially with time)
- Von Bertalanffy-type: dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 - c2 * P (anabolic vs catabolic scaling)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Linear dependence on P (dP_dt proportional to P) → density-independent per-capita growth rate, exponential regime
- Quadratic term in P (P² with negative coefficient) → intraspecific competition or logistic-type density regulation
- Cubic term in P (positive P² and negative P³) → strong Allee effect with both minimum and maximum population thresholds
- Logarithmic function of P (P*log(P)) → Gompertz-type growth where per-capita rate declines logarithmically
- Trigonometric function of t (sin or cos of t) → seasonal or periodic environmental forcing on growth rate
- Ratio P/(1+c*P) → Michaelis-Menten-like resource saturation limiting per-capita growth
- Product P*(P-c) → Allee effect where small populations have negative growth rate
- Exponential function of t multiplied by P → environmental degradation or improvement shifting growth conditions over time
- Fractional power of P (P**c where 0<c<1) → metabolic scaling or allometric growth constraints
- Constant additive term independent of P → immigration/emigration or external population input/removal
